## Governance Analysis

### Key Insights

**Gini Coefficient: 0.9562 (STRONG LOCK)**

- **Strong Lock Signal**: High concentration indicates committed holders are choosing to lock tokens for governance rewards
- **Reduced Sell Pressure**: Most voting power is vested, reducing immediate selling pressure
- **Governance Participation**: Active governance participation by committed stakeholders

**Context**: With 5,000,000+ total EQUAL supply, the concentrated veEQUAL voting power suggests selective participation by holders who value governance rewards over liquidity.

### Distribution Flow

<!-- The flowchart below shows the governance power distribution analysis. -->
```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[Total Holders: 1,707] --> B[Top 1%: 18 holders]

    B --> E[Controls 51.6% of votes]
    C --> F[Controls 88.4% of votes]
    D --> G[Controls 96.4% of votes]
    E --> H[CRITICAL: High governance concentration]
```
